against\n24: // 1. evaluation of ClusterRoleBindings - short circuit on match\n25: // 2. evaluation of RoleBindings in the namespace requested - short circuit on match\n26: // 3. deny by default\n27: \n28: // APIGroupAll and these consts are default values for rbac authorization.\n29: const (\n30: \tAPIGroupAll    = \"*\"\n31: \tResourceAll    = \"*\"\n32: \tVerbAll        = \"*\"\n33: information that describes a policy rule, but does not contain information\n44: // about who the rule applies to or which namespace the rule applies to.\n45: type PolicyRule struct {\n46: \t// Verbs is a list of Verbs that apply to ALL the ResourceKinds contained in this rule. '*' represents all verbs.\n47: \tVerbs []string\n48: \n49: \t// APIGroups is the name of the APIGroup that contains the resources.\n50: \t// If multiple API groups are specified, any action requested against one of the enumerated resources in any API group will be allowed. \"\" represents the core API group and \"*\" represents all API groups.\n51: \tAPIGroups []string\n52: \t// Resources is a list of resources this rule applies to.  '*' represents all resources in the specified apiGroups.\n53: \t// '*/foo' represents the subresource 'foo' for all resources in the specified apiGroups.\n54: \tResources []string\n55: \t// ResourceNames is an optional white list of names that the rule applies to.  An empty set means that everything is allowed.\n56: \tResourceNames []string\n57: \n58: \t// NonResourceURLs is a set of partial urls that a user should have access to.  *s are allowed, but only as the full, final step in the path\n59: \t// If an action is not a resource API request, then the URL is split on '/' and is checked against the NonResourceURLs to look for a match.\n60: \t// Since non-resource URLs are not namespaced, this field is only applicable for ClusterRoles referenced from a ClusterRoleBinding.\n61: \t// Rules can either apply to API resources (such as \"pods\" or \"secrets\") or non-resource URL paths (such as \"/api\"),  but not both.\n62: \tNonResourceURLs []string\n63: }\n64: \n65: // Subject contains a reference to the object or user identities a role binding applies to.  This can either hold a direct API object reference,\n66: // or a value for non-objects such as user and group names.\n67: type Subject struct {\n68: \t// Kind of object being referenced. Values defined by this API group are \"User\", \"Group\", and \"ServiceAccount\".\n69: \t// If the Authorizer does not recognized the kind value, the Authorizer should report an error.\n70: \tKind string\n71: \t// APIGroup holds the API group of the referenced subject.\n72: \t// Defaults to \"\" for ServiceAccount subjects.\n73: \t// Defaults to \"rbac.authorization.k8s.io\" for User and Group subjects.\n74: \tAPIGroup string\n75: \t// Name of the object being referenced.\n76: \tName string\n77: \t// Namespace of the referenced object.  If the object kind is non-namespace, such as \"User\" or \"Group\", and this value is not empty\n78: \t// the Authorizer should report an error.\n79: \tNamespace string\n80: }\n81: \n82: // RoleRef contains information that points to the role being used\n83: type RoleRef struct {\n84: \t// APIGroup is the group for the resource being referenced\n85: \tAPIGroup string\n86: \t// Kind is the type of resource being referenced\n87: \tKind string\n88: \t// Name is the name of resource being referenced\n89: \tName string\n90: }\n91: \n92: // +k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object\n93: \n94: // Role is a namespaced, logical grouping of PolicyRules that can be referenced as a unit by a RoleBinding.\n95: type Role struct {\n96: \tmetav1.TypeMeta\n97: \t// Standard object's metadata.\n98: \tmetav1.ObjectMeta\n99: \n100: \t// Rules holds all the PolicyRules for this Role\n101: \tRules []PolicyRule\n102: }\n103: \n104: // +k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object\n105: \n106: // RoleBinding references a role, but does not contain it.  It can reference a Role in the same namespace or a ClusterRole in the global namespace.\n107: // It adds who information via Subjects and namespace information by which namespace it exists in.  RoleBindings in a given\n108: // namespace only have effect in that namespace.\n109: type RoleBinding struct {\n110: \tmetav1.TypeMeta\n111: \tmetav1.ObjectMeta\n112: \n113: \t// Subjects holds references to the objects the role applies to.\n114: \tSubjects []Subject\n115: \n116: \t// RoleRef can reference a Role in the current namespace or a ClusterRole in the global namespace.\n117: \t// If the RoleRef cannot be resolved, the Authorizer must return an error.\n118: \t// This field is immutable.\n119: \tRoleRef RoleRef\n120: }\n121: \n122: // +k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object\n123: \n124: // RoleBindingList is a collection of RoleBindings\n125: type RoleBindingList struct {\n126: \tmetav1.TypeMeta\n127: \t// Standard object's metadata.\n128: \tmetav1.ListMeta\n129: \n130: \t// Items is a list of roleBindings\n131: \tItems []RoleBinding\n132: }\n133: \n134: // +k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object\n135: \n136: // RoleList is a collection of Roles\n137: type RoleList struct {\n138: \tmetav1.TypeMeta\n139: \t// Standard object's \n148: // ClusterRole is a cluster level, logical grouping of PolicyRules that can be referenced as a unit by a RoleBinding or ClusterRoleBinding.\n149: type ClusterRole struct {\n150: \tmetav1.TypeMeta\n151: \t// Standard object's metadata.\n152: \tmetav1.ObjectMeta\n153: \n154: \t// Rules holds all the PolicyRules for this ClusterRole\n155: \tRules []PolicyRule\n156: \n157: \t//
